 International Driving License is made in Regional Transport Office (RTO)
 International driving license can drive in 150 countries of the world
 If you have an Indian driving license, then you can drive all over India
 lekin agar aap videsh main gaadi chalaanaa chaahate hai, to aapako international driving license banvaanaa hoga
 International driving license is also known as International driving permit
 yah indian driving license kii tarah hi hota he
 International driving license is not a special license
 isko sirf kai bhashaaon main translet kar diya jaataa he
 An International Driving License is obtained within five days of applying to the Regional Transport Office (RTO)
 iske baad aap america, canada, australia samet 150 se zyada deshon main vaahan rent par le sakate hai or driving kar sakate hai
 International driving license can also be used as an identity card abroad
 aapako bataa den ki international driving or road trephic ko lekar antarrashtriya str par bhi kanoon hai
 The 1949 Geneva Convention on Road and Motor Transport and the 1968 Vienna Convention on Road Traffic provide for an International Driving License and International Road Traffic
 aise banavaaen international driving licensesadak parivahan or rajmarg mantralay ke mutabik international driving permit usko jari kiya jaataa he, jiske paas bhartiya driving license ho
 He should also be a resident of India
 iskaa matlab yah he ki agar aapke paas pehle se koi driving license nahin he or aap bharat ke nivasee nahin hai, to aapako international driving license jari nahin kiya jayega
 An International Driving License has to be applied to the Regional Transport Office (RTO) of your area

 jaane phespac lagaate samay kin baton kaa rakhana chahie:1

 2
 Always apply facepack after bathing

 The Ladakh Festival provides an opportunity to showcase its culture, heritage, lifestyle and various castes throughout Ladakh
 yah vishvabhar se paryatakon ko apni ore aakarshith karata he
 The annual Ladakh Festival is held in the city of Leh, Jammu and Kashmir, in the rainbow colors of Ladakh's folk culture amidst the amazing natural landscape of the Himalayan peaks
 15 din tak chalane vaale is mahotsav ke dauraan ladakh kshetra kii sadiyon puraani samskruti, sabhyataa, paramparaon or janajaatiy jivan style kii anupam jhalak dekhne ko milti he
 Traditional songs and music 1
 jammu-kashmir ke paryaton vibhaag dwaara har saal sthaneey samudaayon ke saath milakar 1 se 15 sitambar tak ladakh mahotsav yojit kiya jaataa he
 The festival is organized with the help of local people and Leh and Kargil district administration
 iskaa mukhya uddeshy ko sadiyon puraani ladakh kii saanskrithik paramparaon ko punerjeevit karne or duniya bhar ke logon se iskaa parichay karaane se he
 So that people can connect with this folk heritage, get to know and promote this culture
 2
 a spectacular procession is taken out by various cultural circles of Leh at the opening ceremony of Ladakh Festival
 gaanv ke log paaramparik veshbhusha main bhaag lete hai, geet gaate hai or paaramparik sangeet ke dhun par naachte hai
 Here different types of traditional dances are performed by the participants
 vibhinn prakaar kii pratiyogita1
 Apart from regular programs, interesting archery organized by people around Leh can also be enjoyed here
 saamaajik manyataon ke maddenjar pratibhaagiyon ko apana kaarykram pesh karnaa hota he
 Many programs are organized in this festival

 4

 According to Genesis, there are four types of mountains: (a) Block mountain - When the middle part of the rock falls down due to the fault located in the rocks and the adjacent parts rise up, they are called block mountains
 
 bich main dhanse bhaag ko rift ghati kehete hai
 The top level and the sides of these mountains are confined by sharp debris
 is tarah te parvat ke udhaaharan hai- wasjes (france), blike forest (germany), salt range (pakistan)(b) avshisht parvat (residual mountain)-ye parvat chattaanon ke apradan ke falswarup nirmit hote hai
 Such as Vindhyachal and Satpura, Nilgiris, Parasnath, Rajmahal hills (india), Sierra (spain), Gasa and Bute (america) (c) Accumulated mountains - One of soil, sand, pebbles, stone lava on the crust The mountain which is formed due to accumulating in the place is called accumulated mountain
 registan main banane vaale baaluu ke stupa isi shrenee main aate hai
 (d) Fold mountains - They are formed due to the turning of the surface rocks by the internal forces of the earth
 ye lahardaar parvat hote hai, jinpar asankhya apnatiyaan or abhinatiyaan hoti hai
 Such as - Himalayas, Alps Urals, Rockies and Andes
 (e)valit parvaton ke nirmaan kaa aadhunik sinddhaat plate tectonic (plate Tectonics) kii sankalpana par aadhaarit he
 (f) Where the Himalayan Mountains stand today, at one time there was a huge land legend called Tethys Sagar
 dakshin pathaar ke uttar kii ore visthaapan ke kaaran tethis sagar main bal pad gaye or vah upar uth gaya
 This created the world's highest mountain of the Himalayas
